      <div class="annotation_label">
        
          <h3 class="u-inline">
            About “Oldie”
          </h3>
        
        
      </div>
      <div class="rich_text_formatting">
        <p>The OF posse cut on the mixtape.</p>

<p>To consider Odd Future a viable franchise going forward, listeners needed reminding why they demanded such attention in the first place. Answering the call was the full-on crew record, <em>The OF Tape Vol. 2</em>, capped by the 11-minute mission statement “Oldie”.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="song_metadata u-xx_large_bottom_margin"></div>
    </div>

More on Genius











            About “Oldie”
          


The OF posse cut on the mixtape.
To consider Odd Future a viable franchise going forward, listeners needed reminding why they demanded such attention in the first place. Answering the call was the full-on crew record, The OF Tape Vol. 2, capped by the 11-minute mission statement “Oldie”.










"Oldie" Track Info

Written By

Earl Sweatshirt, Jasper Dolphin, Frank Ocean & 5 more



Label

Odd Future Records, Sony Music & RED Distribution



Recording Engineer

Vic Wainstein



Mixing Engineer

Syd



Mastering Engineer

"Big Bass" Brian Gardner



Vocals

Hodgy, Left Brain, Mike G & 4 more



Release Date
May 12, 2012


Samples


Get out of my life woman by Solomon Burke




Remixed By


Oldie by Traphik


Oldie by Kel Francisco


Old On E. by Blak3d God


OLDIEVERSE by Lewis Shaun


Oldie by JC Ndoci


Oldie (Megamix) by FinnyFromFlickr


Harvest by MASTAMIIND
